```

```

  |                       |               |                               |       |                                       |                       |       |             
(b 3)---(   )---(   )   (   )---(   )---(b 3)   (   )---(   )---(w 3)---(   )   (   )---(   )---(   )   (b 5)---(w 2)---(   )   (   )   (   )   (   )   (   )---(   )
                  |                               |                                               |       |                                       |               |
